  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a452f44b-9f46-4c0f-80ee-46d097d96c41'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer9170243097703138946"><b>From <i>New York Times</i> Bestselling author, Laurelin Paige, <i>Fixed on You</i> is a <i>USA Today</i> Bestseller and Book One in the Trilogy that <i>PEOPLE Magazine</i> named in their Top Ten Reader Favorites of 2014.</b><br/><br/>Fixed on You is the first book in a trilogy but ends without a cliffhanger.   <span id="freeText9170243097703138946" style="display:none"><b>From <i>New York Times</i> Bestselling author, Laurelin Paige, <i>Fixed on You</i> is a <i>USA Today</i> Bestseller and Book One in the Trilogy that <i>PEOPLE Magazine</i> named in their Top Ten Reader Favorites of 2014.</b><br /><br />Fixed on You is the first book in a trilogy but ends without a cliffhanger. Due to mature material, it is recommended for ages 17+.<br /><br />Stalking and restraining orders are a thing of Alayna Wither's past. With her MBA newly in hand, she has her future figured out --move up at the nightclub she works at and stay away from any guy who might trigger her obsessive love disorder. A perfect plan. But what Alayna didn't figure on is Hudson Pierce, the new owner of the nightclub. He's smart, rich, and gorgeous --the kind of guy Alayna knows to stay away from if she wants to keep her past tendencies in check.<br /><br />Except, Hudson's fixed his sights on her. He wants her in his bed and makes no secret of it. Avoiding him isn't an option after he offers a business proposition she can't turn down and she's drawn further into his universe, unable to resist his gravitational pull.<br /><br />When she learns Hudson has a dark history of his own, she realizes too late that she's fallen for the worst man she could possibly get involved with. Or maybe their less than ideal pasts give them an opportunity to heal each other and finally find the love their lives have been missing.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9170243097703138946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

First impression...HOLY SHIT! THIS is what I've been missing! THIS is what everyone has been raving about! Erotic and Intense are just two of the words that describe this series. I could give you a million more, but the FIXED Series by Laurelin Paige is something that you absolutely HAVE TO EXPERIENCE ASAP! DO NOT put this off any longer. It is an absolute MU</span>
  <span id="freeText11115851320333155554" style="display:none">I have had this series on my TBR for what seems like FOREVER! So I decided to put down everything and read the entire series back to back. First impression...HOLY SHIT! THIS is what I've been missing! THIS is what everyone has been raving about! Erotic and Intense are just two of the words that describe this series. I could give you a million more, but the FIXED Series by Laurelin Paige is something that you absolutely HAVE TO EXPERIENCE ASAP! DO NOT put this off any longer. It is an absolute MUST READ for the die hard romance reader in you! Fans of the Crossfire series and other Billionaire Romances will rejoice for Fixed on You. Some elements are the same, the steam factor raised up a notch, but Ms. Paige gave us a fresh new raw romance, following two damaged characters trying to work together to make a relationship work. Alayna will drive you crazy, but in a good way, and Hudson, well...I just have to say...Christian who?<br /><br />Full of intense heat, craziness, and mystery, I wanted nothing more than to bury myself in Hudson's world and NEVER EVER leave! Who knew this would be the start of one of my all time favorite series! God help me, if I was made to wait for the sequel!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11115851320333155554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_678271011" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/678271011" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/678271011?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer678271011" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18202769970520767735"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430706i/863628._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/619539.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b>If dominant and controlling yet tortured heroes make your heart race, then <i> Fixed On You </i> will rock your world!</b><br/><br/>I totally loved this book!!! It gave me that amazing belly fluttering, thrilling feeling of excitement that only my favorite books give me :)<br/><br/>Pretty much my most favorite story line type is flawed or damaged characters working together to try and build a functional relationship while fighting understandable issues but with no stupidity or frustrating behavior and this book ba</span>
  <span id="freeText18202769970520767735" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430706i/863628._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/619539.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br><br><b>If dominant and controlling yet tortured heroes make your heart race, then <i> Fixed On You </i> will rock your world!</b><br><br>I totally loved this book!!! It gave me that amazing belly fluttering, thrilling feeling of excitement that only my favorite books give me :)<br><br>Pretty much my most favorite story line type is flawed or damaged characters working together to try and build a functional relationship while fighting understandable issues but with no stupidity or frustrating behavior and this book basically delivered that to me on a silver platter. I couldn't have been happier - absolute book heaven!<br><br>Fans of the Crossfire series should definitely check this one out! Ever since I'd finished those books, I'd been in withdrawal wishing for another book of that type yet I couldn't find one that quite hit the spot... but this one gave me that same 'intense' feeling and I just reveled in it!<br><br>That being said, it totally stood on it's own as far as the story went. Yes, many of the base points were the same as a lot of the other billionaire stories out there but the details were unique and so it definitely felt like a fresh story.<br><br>The story follows Alayna who, as a result of the circumstances of her past, had developed an <em>obsessive relationship disorder - </em>meaning that she would very easily latch on to relationships and fall in love so much so that she'd strayed into stalker territory at times in her past. It was an issue she was battling and gone to therapy for but she still fought it every day. But she was building her life, had gotten an MBA and was working a great gig at a club bar when the club was suddenly purchased by billionaire Hudson Pierce.<br><br>Hudson was exactly the kind of guy she should stay away from - the kind that would trigger her. Gorgeous, alluring, confident, controlled, dominant. Problem was, he had his sights fixed on her and came to her with an intriguing proposition...<br><br>He wanted to hire her to act as his public girlfriend. He was in a situation that he wanted to get out of and having a girlfriend would sort out all of his problems so he needed to sell the fact that they were in love.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <br>
    <div>
      <em>"This pretend relationship - to what extent would I be expected to perform?"</em>
    </div>
    <br>
    <div>
      <em>"Don't pussy foot about it. You're asking about sex." His eyes darkened again. "I never pay for sex, Alayna. When I fuck you, it will be for free."</em>
    </div>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Granted, Alayna was understandably wary of the proposition at first knowing full well that it would just feed into her compulsion making it even harder for her to not latch on emotionally and it didn't help that Hudson's interest with her was not solely professional...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>"I apologize for overwhelming you. That wasn't my intent. But I want you to know that whether or not you decide to help with my situation, I will continue to seduce you. I'm a man who gets what he wants. And I want you."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And he was also harboring dark secrets from his past that made him almost incapable of love...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"First, let me clear up one thing… I will be saying and doing things - romantic things, perhaps - that are not genuine. I need you to remember that. Out of the public eye, I will seduce you. That will be genuine, but it can never be misconstrued as love."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em> "Because you're incapable of love." …</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em> "Yes."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>... but despite all of this, their attraction and feelings were real and even her issues and his secrets couldn't keep them apart :)<br><br>I absolutely adored Hudson. He was the kind of guy that makes my heart <em>race. </em>He was alluring and yet contradictory. He remained distant and aloof while at the same time he seemed totally infatuated with her. But I'm just such a sucker for the controlled yet tortured heroes.... they make my heart melt every time and Hudson was no exception.<br><br>I honestly wasn't sure how I'd feel about Alayna at first given what I knew about her obsession but I ended up liking that it made her flawed because while she was very aware of her limitations and while it made her wary of their relationship, I liked that she had something real she was struggling with.<br><br>I also have to say that I absolutely <em>loved</em> that while Alayna did have issues, she wasn't broken and she certainly wasn't a pushover by any means. The scenes with her facing off with Hudson's mother were just awesome! Here's just a little taste...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Tell me, Alayna - were you first attracted to my son because of his money or his name?"<br><br>Pissed didn't even begin to describe how I felt. I was seething, but in control. Without skipping a beat, I wrapped my arm around Hudson's arm and answered. "Neither. I was attracted to him because he's hot. Though, I stayed with him because he's fucking awesome in bed."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>So she had issues, he had secrets, and their relationship was a sham but somehow it all just worked.<br><br>There were so many times when you'd wonder... how much of what was going on between them was for show and how much of it was real feelings developing? Where was the line? When did it begin to blur?<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"If I wondered that the whole act was a display... his whisper in my ear said otherwise, "This, precious. This is for real."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>There's just something about characters with deep problems actually trying to work through them in a functional way that just makes my heart happy. I loved that I never once rolled my eyes or wanted to throttle either Alayna or Hudson. Yes, they both messed up on occasion. No, neither of them were perfect. But... I loved that I could sense that they both did want to make things work and because of that, I loved reading about their ups and downs.<br><br>And as the story progressed, their connection deepened and it wasn't just a physical connection, they were a match in intelligence too and because of their dark pasts, they both found things in each other that they could sympathize with.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I turned to him and found his gaze absent of pity. Instead it held understanding. More and more I realized that I was special to him because of this unique recognition he saw in me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>This book also kept me smiling and fanning myself. It wasn't light-hearted but it was a lot of <em>fun! </em>There were some total shocking moments, some laugh-out-loud moments and boat loads of <em>hotness</em> but the heart of it was what drew me in. For a good chunk of the time I was reading, I had that delicious butterflies-in-my-belly feeling. It was hot, thrilling, and engaging. I really loved it :)<br><br>This is the kind of book that gets better as it goes along though. In the beginning, for the first 40% or so, I was sitting at a comfortable 4-star rating. I liked it but was waiting for that extra 'spark' and then just the pieces really started to come together until by the end, I was pretty much at 5-star love. So I'm going to round it off to a very happy 4.5 star rating.<br><br>Oh, and I seriously just want to hug the author for not leaving this book on a cliffhanger. I really mean it. Despite this being the first book in a trilogy, there is <u>no cliffhanger</u>!! Nothing. Not even a dark something from the past that creeps in or anything. I mean sure there is more of their story to tell but it was like the author totally trusted that you'd want to read the next book of your own accord and you know what?? I TOTALLY DO!!!!!<br><br>All in all, this book pushed all the right buttons for me. I loved the characters, cared for them, and wanted to see them work their issues out. Not to mention that this book has some serious hotness in it - I mean... that's what you get with a dominant, controlling hero *grins* ... so overall, it took a little while in the beginning for this book to fully capture my heart but once it did, it didn't let go and kept it through 'til the very end.<br><br><b> This is definitely the start of a new favorite series for me. <em>Fixed On You</em> is the first book in a trilogy but again, no cliffhanger! You're totally safe to go ahead and read this now!<br><br>*squee*<br><br>4.5 stars </b><br><br><i> The sequel, Found In You, will be released on October 1st, 2013 and will continue Hudson and Alayna's story. </i><br><br>My casting:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430706i/863629._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430706i/863630._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1368076802l/17828418.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Stalking and restraining orders are a thing of Alayna Wither’s past. With her MBA newly in hand, she has her future figured out—move up at the nightclub she works at and stay away from any guy who might trigger her obsessive love disorder. A perfect plan.<br><br>But what Alayna didn’t figure on is Hudson Pierce, the new owner of the nightclub. He’s smart, rich, and gorgeous—the kind of guy Alayna knows to stay away from if she wants to keep her past tendencies in check. Except, Hudson’s fixed his sights on her. He wants her in his bed and makes no secret of it.<br><br>Avoiding him isn’t an option after he offers a business proposition she can’t turn down and she’s drawn further into his universe, unable to resist his gravitational pull. When she learns Hudson has a dark history of his own, she realizes too late that she’s fallen for the worst man she could possibly get involved with. Or maybe their less than ideal pasts give them an opportunity to heal each other and finally find the love their lives have been missing. </i><br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/676903122?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer676903122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5808170161259705732"><a href='http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/07/blog-tour-fixed-on-you-by-laurelin.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>This review is posted on Angie's Dreamy Reads!</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430510i/863120.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>One word ladies....Hudson!!! Hudson -panty sizzler- Pierce. He is absolutely delectable. Sexy, rich, dominating, swoon worthy, arrogant, damaged, fanfuckingtastic. He's sex on a stick. That's what he is! He oozes manly yumminess! I didn't just love this book, I freaking <b>ADORED</b> and <b>DEVOURED</b> it. It wasn't too angsty, overly dramatic or intense. It was just perfect. It took you away to that "happy place" and kept you there and when it was over you were </span>
  <span id="freeText5808170161259705732" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/07/blog-tour-fixed-on-you-by-laurelin.html" rel="nofollow noopener">This review is posted on Angie's Dreamy Reads!</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430510i/863120.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One word ladies....Hudson!!! Hudson -panty sizzler- Pierce. He is absolutely delectable. Sexy, rich, dominating, swoon worthy, arrogant, damaged, fanfuckingtastic. He's sex on a stick. That's what he is! He oozes manly yumminess! I didn't just love this book, I freaking <b>ADORED</b> and <b>DEVOURED</b> it. It wasn't too angsty, overly dramatic or intense. It was just perfect. It took you away to that "happy place" and kept you there and when it was over you were screaming, <b>
  <i>NO, NO, NO, **waving your kindle in the air** this can't, just can't be over..whyyyyyy! I NEED MORE!!!</i>
</b> ** Insert dramatic face** He's what I'd call my perfect book husband. This is the man you dream and fantasize about. He makes every page on your eReader sizzle. It’s a no brainer 5 star read for me. There's not one single damn thing I'd change. Not one. It was captivating, steamy and made my little heart thump, thump, thump. I love being whisked away by a rich, damaged, sexy alpha male while being seduced one delicious, scrumptious word at a time. I think I honestly became Laynie when I read this..no joke. It was a complete possession...hahaha! Ok, ok I'm getting a bit melodramatic but I can't help it. This book owned me when I read it. It's been awhile since I've read a book as hot as Damien Stark, Gideon Cross or Bennett Ryan. A book that just tantalizes and teases every single part of you. I love these kinds of reads. I want to escape in the pages and leave all my worries, stresses and day to day troubles behind. This book did that. It took me away from my everyday life and made me <b>NEVER</b> want to return. <br><br>Laynie is a very damaged girl. She has some stalker tendencies **insert smirk** , which I found very in endearing. Maybe that makes me insane, but this girl has major family issues and the way she deals with them is by latching on to men. That has earned her quite a bit of trouble in the past. She works at a bar and after counseling she is pretty much walking the straight and narrow. Laynie has her sights set on a management position at The Sky Launch bar and is working her way up to the top. David her current hook up and boss is Laynie’s ticket to what she thinks she wants <b>BUT</b> the bar is sold to a new owner and Laynie’s chance to get that promotion might be a little delayed. <br><br>Hudson Pierce is the new owner of The Sky Launch bar. A wealthy, arrogant and sexy businessman, he has his eyes set on Laynie and it’s a little more than meets the eye. Hudson is a man who <b>ALWAYS,</b> and I mean <b>ALWAYS</b> get what he wants. And this time he needs Laynie to do a job for him. It’s not your typical proposition but comes at the perfect time for Laynie because the life she’s worked hard to build is slowly fizzling away. With an offer too good to refuse and a sexual chemistry too intense to deny Laynie says <b>YES</b> to a proposal that is <b>SURE</b> to change her life. <br><br>Together Hudson and Laynie are <b>SCORCHING.</b> The sexual tension they ooze is palpable. This book is <b>FUN, ENJOYABLE</b> and <b>DAMN SEXY.</b> The best part is that Laynie and Hudson are both fantastic characters. Laynie is definitely a lovable, sweet girl. One that I fell in love with. I didn't just love this book because of Huds...No, I loved it because Laynie was a bad ass chick too. She made me feel for her, connect to her and her issues. I loved being in her mind, listening to her thoughts and experiencing her feelings for Huds. The characters are <b>AMAZING.</b> Really they both rocked. <br><br>Hudson...Well I told you above! He is <b>EVERYTHING</b> you could want. I love a billionaire, alpha male that takes what he wants and asks questions later. That is my perfect man and Hudson filled every trait. <br><br>I would recommend this if you are a fan of Beautiful Bastard, Bared to You and Release Me. This book is in the same category. It’s one HOT read, sure to tug on your heart, wet your panties **wink wink** and make you swoon. Get ready for a ride you won’t <b>EVER</b> want to end.<br><br>MY BLOG LINK --&gt;&gt; <a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Angie's Dreamy Reads</a><br><br>BLOG FACEBOOK LINK ---&gt;&gt; <a href="https://www.facebook.com/AngiesDreamyReads" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook - Angie's Dreamy Reads</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1830107892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9304458551390981885"><b>Ms Paige writes unique, flawed characters and while- in principle- Alayna and Hudson</b> were written perfectly, I neither got sucked in nor did I particularly care about their story. That notwithstanding, I probably will read the next serial.</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11095761435697973377"><b>4 Deliciously Flawed Stars<br/><br/><i>”In his words, in his actions, I felt fixed. I’d fallen into something that had nothing to do with love. Into healing. And it was love too. If I could stand to admit it to myself, love was exactly what it was.”</i></b><br/><br/>Love heals and sooths. It fixes and sets wrongs straight. Have faith in love and trust your feelings. When everything else fails, they will not betray you.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400868i/777325.png' width='400' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We are far from perfect. Vindictive and lying bastards, scared, wounded people with pasts and a ton of emotio</span>
  <span id="freeText11095761435697973377" style="display:none"><b>4 Deliciously Flawed Stars<br><br><i>”In his words, in his actions, I felt fixed. I’d fallen into something that had nothing to do with love. Into healing. And it was love too. If I could stand to admit it to myself, love was exactly what it was.”</i></b><br><br>Love heals and sooths. It fixes and sets wrongs straight. Have faith in love and trust your feelings. When everything else fails, they will not betray you.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400868i/777325.png" width="400" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We are far from perfect. Vindictive and lying bastards, scared, wounded people with pasts and a ton of emotional baggage to sort through. Our heads are a mess, but are our hearts can’t be closed off forever. Along comes someone, similarly scarred that knock us off our feet when we are least expecting it.<br><br>Love is what we have been searching for, for eternities. Wars have been fought and cities where destroyed in its name. Who are we really to believe that we can escape? How can we deny the other half of our soul, when it stares us right in the eyes and is begging us for a chance at happiness? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427957i/855801.jpg" width="400" height="231" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fear and arrogance are the worst bed-mates. They bleed poison in your soul while wrapping you in cotton, supposedly to protect you. Empty affairs, floozy sex partners, dysfunctional families. They seem a lot to overcome but the end will reward you and you got to try, even playing dirty, by any means necessary. <br><br>Perfect is overrated and normal is frankly quite boring. Head cases are the new sexy and *orgasm alert* ladies, they will blow you away! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405518i/790041.jpg" width="400" height="462" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”I’d like to pay you to help me with a problem. I believe you’d be perfect for the job.” <br>“You win. My curiosity is piqued. What’s the job?” <br>“I need you to break up an engagement.” <br>“Um, what? Whose?”<br>Hudson leaned back, his dazzling gray eyes flickering in the strobe lights. “Mine.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427957ra/855802.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>SHRILL FANGIRLING SCREAMS</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427957ra/855803.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427957ra/855804.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Alayna Laynie Withers</b> is trying to move on with her life after picking up the pieces of her broken shelf. The girl who lost her parents, was raised by her unloving and simply bastard brother had once tried to find the love and partnership it was denied to her in relationships. But she couldn’t be normal. She was latching on, fixating and getting worked up on guys, until a restraining order put her straight. Having earned her business degree and trying to make the most out of her job in a high-end bar, she mistakenly thinks that sleeping with the right man will give her the place she deserves. Vulnerable and wounded, she will catch the eye of a man so dangerous to her mindset that will shake all her beliefs and will open her eyes to whole new world of sensual pleasure and emotional stability. That is until they admit what they mean to each other…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427957i/855805.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Hudson Pierce</b> a ruthless businessman, an attractive and arrogant man is the new owner of the nightclub. He needs to set up quickly an elaborate façade to fool everyone and not end up married to a woman he doesn’t want. He propositions Alayna; a sham relationship and sex with no strings. All the pleasure she can handle. In exchange he will pay off her student loans. They just have to fool everyone, especially his total BITCH of a mother, that they are desperately in love and not fall for each other in the process. Piece of cake, right? NOT!<br><br>A man incapable of loving and a woman that loves too much. Will they make it? Will they go against the odds and end up with a love of a lifetime? Or fear and cowardice, will forever be holding them hostage?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427957i/855806.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><pre>HOLY SMOCKING HOTNESS!</pre><br>Sexy, unapologetic, twisted, fun and exciting, full of intense dialogue, funny banter between the characters and a delight to read and fantasize about sex scenes, this book will keep your eyes glued to the page, making you crazy with the heroes antics and inability or maybe unwillingness to face the truth and admit what is obvious to anyone with eyes and functioning reproductive organs.<br>THEY ARE PERFECT FOR EACH OTHER!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427957ra/855807.gif" width="400" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Small cliffie, no big deal, just makes the sequel all more anticipating. I freaking can’t wait!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409147ra/800905.gif" width="400" height="226" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Maja</b>, hon, thank you very much, for a great recommendation!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/529703.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

I can’t believe I waited to so long to pick up this series!<br><br>Alayna has a problem, she kind of loves too hard. Whenever she gets into a relationship with a guy, she goes overboard, into stalkerish territory. Hudson is a successful, sexy business man who doesn’t know how to love, but he needs to get his mom off his back. Hudson makes a deal with Alayna. If Alayna can pretend to be his girlfriend to get his mom off his back, then he will pay for Alayna’s school debt. Alayna desperately wants to get out of debt, but she is afraid she may fall for Hudson because of her problem.<br><br>The blurb is really adorable. I actually had no idea what Fixed on You was about, for some reason, I thought Alayna was like a sex addict or something. I haven’t read a “cutesy” book in a very long time and I forget how much I miss these kinds of reads.<br><br>The relationship between Hudson and Alayna is very cute, there’s a little tension and banter too. You do not have to wait too long to get to the steam and no there’s no “insta-love”, but definitely “insta-lust” and I’m ALL FOR THAT. <br><br>I love the alpha billionaire-story line, it’s probably one of my top favorites and Paige really surprised me on how unique the characters were. I’ve never read a character where the Heroine falls too quickly in love, it was very comical and different. Hudson is the typical rich, sexy, play-boy, but honestly there’s nothing to complain about, because he hits the mark.<br><br>Fixed on You is a quick, light and very steamy read. I recommend completely. There is also a HEA, so don’t worry, no cliffy.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25967039-fixed-on-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=re-reads">re-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=boxset">boxset</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=audible-owned">audible-owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=my-kind-of-alpha">my-kind-of-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1656656424" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14323009665474601816"><b>Audible Review:</b><br/>Distinguishable between characters: 5 Stars<br/>Impersonating opposite sex: 4 Stars<br/>Accents: n/a<br/>Overall enjoyment of Performance: 5 Stars. <br/>Recommend audible version: Yes<br/><br/><b>Story Review:</b> When I got this book 2 years ago, this was an unknown author to me. I actually didn't know many authors since I was stuck in the HR phase up until that point. This book just happened to be one of the first freebies I came across on Amazon and I thought why not give it a try. I'm so glad that I did. This ser</span>
  <span id="freeText14323009665474601816" style="display:none"><b>Audible Review:</b><br />Distinguishable between characters: 5 Stars<br />Impersonating opposite sex: 4 Stars<br />Accents: n/a<br />Overall enjoyment of Performance: 5 Stars. <br />Recommend audible version: Yes<br /><br /><b>Story Review:</b> When I got this book 2 years ago, this was an unknown author to me. I actually didn't know many authors since I was stuck in the HR phase up until that point. This book just happened to be one of the first freebies I came across on Amazon and I thought why not give it a try. I'm so glad that I did. This series has turned out to be one of my top favorites, even two years later. <br /><br />I will admit that this first book in the series started out real iffy for me. I do not like needy females and I want a story that has the man chasing the woman. When I found out that Alayna was a reformed stalker...well I had a hard time with her behavior. She kinda came of crazy in this first book. <br /><br />The real reason I stuck through her crazy, was Hudson. Hudson came off kinda mysterious and frankly that intrigued me. When we find out Hudson has his own issues, instead of turning me off the story, it just hooked me more. I needed to see where this was going. <br /><br />This is not a low angst book. On top of Alayna and Hudson's own brand of crazy, we get Hudson's train wreck of a family, and then there is his friend Celia. There is something going on with Celia and it's not good. She's fishy and I know I'm going to want to push her off a cliff.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14323009665474601816" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1374736711" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1374736711" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1374736711?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25967039-fixed-on-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=alphaboys">alphaboys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1374736711" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15859963948887849131"><i>
  <b>"...you’re looking for something temporary. Something fun to play with.” I leaned even closer to deliver my punch line—the one that would deter even the horniest of men. “And I get attached.” I stood back up to my full height so I could take in his reaction. “Now doesn’t that just scare you shitless?”<br/><br/>I’d expected to see panic flash through his face. Instead, I saw a flicker of amusement. “You, Alayna Withers, do anything but scare me.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>Alayna is one of my most favourite girls and this is one </span>
  <span id="freeText15859963948887849131" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"...you’re looking for something temporary. Something fun to play with.” I leaned even closer to deliver my punch line—the one that would deter even the horniest of men. “And I get attached.” I stood back up to my full height so I could take in his reaction. “Now doesn’t that just scare you shitless?”<br /><br />I’d expected to see panic flash through his face. Instead, I saw a flicker of amusement. “You, Alayna Withers, do anything but scare me.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Alayna is one of my most favourite girls and this is one of my favourite romance series. <br />Alayna is different. She is definitely not like the rest of the main female characters in the romance novels. She is NOT normal. She is not stupid. Some people may say that she is crazy. But she is just extraordinary and unique. She knows what she wants, she knows how this will end up and she stays away.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’m going to rock your world”</i>
</b><br /><br />In this story I really preferred the female character and I was at her side supporting her all the way, while I wanted to punch Hudson's face and make him bleed from the first time we met him in book 1 until the last page in book 3 -although, book 3 is another story, full of twists.<br /><br />Alanea is a survivor. She has her personal psychological problems like obsession with old boyfriends and she will possibly be obsessed with any future boyfriends. She also has low self esteem. They had press charges against her in the past and now she has been under restricting order. She fights against her obsessions and her herself. She wins so far. She has decided that she will never be obsessed again with anybody. She will never fall in love. Only sex, she will never give heart and soul.<br /><br />On the other hand there is Hudson, a rich playboy who is a maestro in breaking hearts. Because he is a sociopath. He knows it. Everybody knows it. He has had professional help about this problem. He admits it to Alanea. At the same time he has a proposition for her. It is simple: <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“What exactly would you want me to do?”<br /><br />“Pretend we’re a couple. I’d invite you to several gatherings where my mother would see us together. I’d expect you to hang on my arm and behave as though we’re madly in love.”<br /><br />“And that’s all?”</b>
</i><br /><br />That way his family will leave him and in return he will pay all Alayna's student loans. Moreover he warns her that he hurts people and he is incapable of loving anybody.<br /><br />Alayna needs the money and she also likes what she sees and so she agrees. It is only a game after all and plain sex. Nobody will get hurt. She has made a promise to herself that she will never fall in love.<br /><br /><u>A guy who cannot love and a girl who always loves too much, more than she should.</u><br />This is the recipe for lots of angst.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“No romance? I can do that.”<br /><br />Hudson leaned back on the front of his desk again. He raised a brow, amusement in his eyes. “Are you also incapable of love?”<br /><br />I met his gaze and ignored the little voice in my head telling me to run. “No, just the opposite. I love too much. Keeping love out of the equation is a very good thing.”<br /><br />“Good. No love.”</i>
</b><br /><br />And then the lies begin and the secrets. And then more lies and more secrets and more lies on top of the lies.<br /><br />I admit that there is a happy ending in the book. Everybody is happy. A brand new beginning for everyone. But then you already know there is a second book. And your stomach hurts a bit because you have a really bad feeling about the things that will follow...Hudson is still around after all.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“We’re really doing this, aren’t we? Moving forward.”<br /><br />“We are.”</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15859963948887849131" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20809413-fixed-on-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=freebie">freebie</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2980038590" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15799657607413895693"><b>4.5 Double Head Case Stars</b><br/><br/>Wow... where to begin with this one...? As the title of this review alludes to, both of these characters have some not so small psychological issues. Alayna ("Laynie" to her friends) has just completed her MBA degree and is celebrating her success at the night club where she has been employed for several years. While most people would look for a 9-5 type of corporate job, Laynie enjoys the industry and wants to move up the management ladder by sharing some new ideas she</span>
  <span id="freeText15799657607413895693" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Double Head Case Stars</b><br /><br />Wow... where to begin with this one...? As the title of this review alludes to, both of these characters have some not so small psychological issues. Alayna ("Laynie" to her friends) has just completed her MBA degree and is celebrating her success at the night club where she has been employed for several years. While most people would look for a 9-5 type of corporate job, Laynie enjoys the industry and wants to move up the management ladder by sharing some new ideas she has for improving the club. As she takes a celebratory shot with her friends who also work there, she sees a customer she has never seen before at the end of the bar... and when she gets closer, her panties steam up. He is everything she has sworn to avoid in a man: dominant, gorgeous, confident, and wealthy. But as the bartender on duty, she has to take his order (single malt scotch, neat.... of course). After he tips her a ridiculous amount that she tries to give back, he leaves... and she is relieved as he is anything but safe for her. Laynie has a tendency to go overboard in her relationships, and by overboard, let's just say that there have been restraining orders and law suits. She tends to get quickly attached, and now that she has been in therapy for a few years, she knows it is most likely related to her childhood wherein her parents were killed when she was young, and her older brother took over as a parent, though he was not very supportive or loving. This has led Laynie to seek male approval and security in her romantic relationships, and though she has been issue-free for years now, she knows the mystery man at the bar would most likely tailspin her back to her obsessive days.<br /><br />Hudson Pierce gets what he wants, and right now what he wants is Alayna. He saw her present her thesis project where he was a judge/panelist, and she is everything he likes in a woman: brunette, large-chested, gorgeous, and smart. She is the perfect person for him to hire to pretend to be his girlfriend to get his mother off his back as she has been bullying him into marrying the daughter of her best friend with whom he has no attraction to or interest in beyond friendship. Laynie, the bartender of the club he has just acquired as a "hot, young billionaire CEO" of {insert generic sounding name here} company, is his type to a T, which is why he is certain she will be convincing in the role of gf who has earned his ever-loving devotion and will release him from any obligation his mother has attempted to entangle him in. And while Hudson believes he is incapable of love, he 100% wants to get it on with Laynie behind-the-scenes. But how can that possibly work between a couple where one cannot connect and the other over-connects? What happens when the line between the pretend and the real starts to blur?<br /><br />What I liked:<br />--- Hudson is a mega alpha male - yum!<br />--- Laynie is a gorgeous woman, but she is super flawed which makes her feel way more relatable<br />--- STEAMY goodness!<br /><br />What I didn't like as much:<br />--- Sometimes there is way more angst than necessary, but the author mostly resolves those issues quickly (meaning miscommunication is rarely the problem, or if it is, it isn't for long)<br />--- It left me dangling ---- ahhhh!!! Cliffhanger alert!<br /><br />Overall, a delicious read with plenty of steam, twists, and strong plot line. (And, of course, I had to go and get the next book!)<br /><br />Plot --- 4.5/5<br />Main Characters --- 4.5/5<br />Supporting Cast --- 4/5<br />Steam Level* --- 4/5<br />Violence --- none<br />Language --- the f word makes appearances early &amp; often<br />POV --- 1st (Laynie's POV)<br /><br />*Note that steam level is not a rating so much as a how hot was it: 0/5 - clean; 1/5 - mild; 2/5 - sensual but nothing descriptive; 3/5 - now we're getting somewhere; 4/5 - yes please! ; 5/5 - they did EVERYTHING in this one, y'all</span>
  <a data-text-id="15799657607413895693" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_644530238" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/644530238" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5107700-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371826269p2/5107700.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/644530238?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/5107700-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer644530238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4258154540605922442"><b>Alayna</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425833i/850164._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Alayna is working as a bar tender at a bar called The Sky Launch. One night while working she turns to find a HOT stranger watching her or as her friend/cowoker Lisel describes him as “midnight masturbation material “. When their eyes meet there is instant sexual attraction between them. Later she finds out that the hot stranger is actually the new owner of the bar and her boss, Hudson Pierce.<br/><br/><b>Hudson</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425833i/850165._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Hudson Pierce is a total alpha male that always gets what he wants. He’s also the type of gu</span>
  <span id="freeText4258154540605922442" style="display:none"><b>Alayna</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425833i/850164._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alayna is working as a bar tender at a bar called The Sky Launch. One night while working she turns to find a HOT stranger watching her or as her friend/cowoker Lisel describes him as “midnight masturbation material “. When their eyes meet there is instant sexual attraction between them. Later she finds out that the hot stranger is actually the new owner of the bar and her boss, Hudson Pierce.<br><br><b>Hudson</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425833i/850165._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hudson Pierce is a total alpha male that always gets what he wants. He’s also the type of guy that brings out all of the obsessive tendencies in Alayna and she knows it. Hudson decides that Alayna is the perfect person who can help him with a problem so he confronts her.<br><br><b>“I’d like to pay you to help me with a problem I believe you’d be perfect for the job.”<br><br>The whole conversation had my head spinning, but he had my attention. “You win. My curiosity is piqued. What’s the job?”<br><br>“I need you to break up an engagement.”<br><br>“Whose?”<br><br>He leaned back, his dazzling gray eyes flickering in the strobe lights.<br><br>“Mine.”</b><br><br>Hudson offers to pay off all of Alayna’s student loans if she helps convince his family and friends that he’s in love with her. Little does she know that he has secrets of his own, Hudson is not capable of love. Both struggle not to let their addictions not take over in this charade. <br><br><b>“I will be saying and doing things— romantic things, perhaps— that are not genuine. <br><br>I need you to remember that. Out of the public eye, I will seduce you. <br><br>That will be genuine, but it can never be misconstrued as love.”<br></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425833i/850166._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As they both do their best to put on the best show they can, the lines soon become blurred and feelings are involved. <br><br><b>I sensed the warning in Hudson’s face, but I couldn’t stop myself from saying more. “We’re falling in love. This is us, falling in love.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425833i/850167._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved this story and cannot wait to see where the future takes Alayna and Hudson. The second book, “Found in You” is scheduled to come out in October 2013.<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14881910789856808508">This was a really interesting book. In many ways, it's like 100 books I've read before. Rich guy, "poor" girl, an "arrangement" - However, Laurelin Page put a twist on it that has me hooked. <br/><br/>Hudson and Alayna both have issues. BIG issues. Issues that had me biting my fingernails through out the book just waiting for one of them to go over the edge. Yet somehow, their own personal neurosis, which should have made them just about the worse possible match, seem to work. At least so far. <br/><br/>I haven't s</span>
  <span id="freeText14881910789856808508" style="display:none">This was a really interesting book. In many ways, it's like 100 books I've read before. Rich guy, "poor" girl, an "arrangement" - However, Laurelin Page put a twist on it that has me hooked. <br /><br />Hudson and Alayna both have issues. BIG issues. Issues that had me biting my fingernails through out the book just waiting for one of them to go over the edge. Yet somehow, their own personal neurosis, which should have made them just about the worse possible match, seem to work. At least so far. <br /><br />I haven't spent so much time googling while reading a book since I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12368985.Consequences__Consequences___1_" title="Consequences (Consequences, #1) by Aleatha Romig" rel="nofollow noopener">Consequences</a>. I want to meet Ms. Page just so I can ask her where she got this idea from. I'm totally intrigued by both of the main characters, and I'm fascinated by how this is all moving forward. <br /><br />For those of you, who like me, cannot stand a cliffhanger, you are probably safe reading this one. While the story is far from over (and my stomach is in knots just thinking about all the things that could go horribly wrong in a permanently psychologically scaring way) it ends in a satisfying place which won't have you tearing your hair out. <br /></span>

<div id="review_601702978" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/601702978" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412857185p2/13978199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/601702978?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review">arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=angsty-romance">angsty-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer601702978" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4282657416929384131">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>5 <b> “precious” </b> Kisses!<br/><br/>My heart is full. Very full. Of love. Of promise. Of possibilities. That is what this book has brought me. Oh…and because I’m a dirty book whore, my heart is full of lust. Because jeez louise as much as this book angst’d the crap out of my heart, it equally filled it up with desire and longing…and horniness. Just sayin’… I really had no idea where this book was going to take me, but <b>wow</b> am I more than pleasantly surprised. I couldn’t put</span>
  <span id="freeText4282657416929384131" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>5 <b> “precious” </b> Kisses!<br><br>My heart is full. Very full. Of love. Of promise. Of possibilities. That is what this book has brought me. Oh…and because I’m a dirty book whore, my heart is full of lust. Because jeez louise as much as this book angst’d the crap out of my heart, it equally filled it up with desire and longing…and horniness. Just sayin’… I really had no idea where this book was going to take me, but <b>wow</b> am I more than pleasantly surprised. I couldn’t put this book down, read it in less than a day. Devoured it because that’s what it did to me. It devoured me…mind, body and soul, and I couldn’t get enough! I’m begging for more! Give me more Hudson!!! *deep calming breaths*<br><br>Alayna ‘Laynie’ Withers…she’s a 26 year old bombshell with long brown hair and actual brains to go along with all those good looks. She’s graduating with her MBA from Stern…yet she’s a bit of a contradiction because while some would be looking for a job in the field where you get your degree from, Laynie is quite alright staying right where she is…working as a bartender at The Sky Launch Nightclub. But that’s a different issue….of course she’s a catch, she has to be to garner the eye of a certain über rich mogul, but beneath the gorgeous exterior lies a mentally troubled girl. The death of her parents when she was younger left her in a fragile state. Something that wasn’t handled as quickly as it should have been. She was raised by her older brother, leaving their relationship in less than stellar shape because who wants to have to deal with a teenage girl with ‘issues’. But the past is in the past, Laynie is making progress…until he sits down at her bar.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419319i/831148._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ‘“I so got this.” I so didn’t have it. Not with Mr. Draw-Laynie-To-Me-Whatever-The-Cost-To-Her-Sanity sitting at the end of the bar.’ </b><br><br>Hudson Pierce – Mr. All Business, Mr. No Emotions, Mr. Holy-shit-you’re-so-freaking-hot-just-screw-me. Hmm…may have gotten carried away with that one. He’s 29 with floppy brown hair and intense grey eyes that just scream ‘fuck me’…or maybe I just screamed that while I was reading about him. There is just something about a dark, brooding, self-contained businessman that just does it for me in all kinds of delicious ways, and Hudson Pierce did that. Very well. It wasn't just all those good looks and sex appeal that did it for me, there <i>is</i> more to Hudson, I promise. He's successful and intelligent and says <b>the</b> most drool worthy things, but when you combine all that in such a steamy package...well, that's just kryptonite for me. :-) So...there’s a…'deal' if you will, I don’t wanna spoil the deal because that was the jaw drop moment for me and I’d hate to steal that from someone. I didn't see it coming...and I loved it.<br><br><b> ‘He lowered his head to my ear. “Wait, Alayna.” His breath tickled and burned simultaneously. I closed my eyes, taking it in, bearing it. “I apologize for overwhelming you. That wasn’t my intent. But I want you to know that whether or not you decide to help with my situation, I will continue to seduce you. I’m a man who gets what he wants. And I want you.” <br><i> Um, holy wow.</i> <br>Turned on did not begin to describe how his statement made me feel.’ </b><br><br>So welcome to the world of ‘girl with obsessive issues’ meets ‘boy with love and commitment issues’…two people with <i> ‘less than ideal pasts’ </i> that you really shouldn’t want to be together, but damn it, they’re just so flippin’ perfect for each other. He and Laynie have a lot in common in the mental issues department. She loves too much, to the point of obsession and he doesn’t love at all. It’s sex with Hudson…take it or leave – and GOD Bless America, does Laynie ever take it. But seriously, it’s better to have Hudson than to not have him at all. You couldn’t put a better couple together than Alayna (because he doesn’t call her Laynie) and H (her nick name for him….and yes I think it’s the cutest thing on the planet). I can’t lie…the physical aspect of their relationship hooked me first. Hello…this would be a red alert on the ‘panty melting’ – like sweet Mary, Joseph and baby Jesus did this book set me on fire. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419319ra/831149.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> He let out a brief laugh, as if he recognized his own vulnerability and it amused him or confounded him. “I’m drawn to you, Alayna. Not because I want to hurt you or make you feel a certain way, but because you’re beautiful and sexy and smart and, yes, a little crazy, maybe, but you’re not broken. And that makes me hopeful. <i>For me</i>.” </b><br><br>I have no shame, clearly, with what I am about to say…this book had me panting. I could feel their chemistry. It was electric. Their connection, their desire, all of it was just so…freaking….<b>
  <i>HOT</i>
</b>! I couldn’t get enough. They might be able to deny soooo many things, their feelings, the reality of the situation, anything else – but the one thing they cannot deny is their physical attraction to each other and the fact that they are sexually <b>very</b> compatible. This book is in it’s own category in my brain because the sex scenes were worthy of an erotica book, but the plot, writing, characters, everything else was 100% contemporary romance…it was an amazingly well meshed blend. And there <i>is</i> so much more to this book than all the hotness...there's Hudson's evil mother (I'm not exaggerating...she is evil), the possibly evil 'friend' Celia...there's drama with Laynie's brother...so, it's not all smooth sailing and hot sex...but I tell you that's why it hooked me! If I wasn't all tied up in knots over angst, I was gasping for breath over the sexual chemistry between these two. Win/Win if you ask me!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419319ra/831150.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ‘He labeled it as a kiss for our distant spectators, but it was completely ours—a harmonic blending of him and me, so thoroughly fused I could no longer remember where he began, where I ended, whose taste belonged to who. And it was more—a love song without words, a promise without fear. It was a spark, a beginning of something new.’ </b><br><br>Holy crap do I need their sequel. God Bless Miss. Paige for not cliffing me, which I thought she might do there for a hot second, but she didn’t…so they’re happy, I’m happy…but we could all be happier. I need my ‘finality’ with them, they’ve worked very hard to get where they are and now they need a conclusion. A beautiful one, that I may have already dreamed up in my imagination – but I have a feeling the actual version will be a million times better. I have yet to be anything less than thrilled to bits with what I have read…I doubt <i> Found In You </i> will be anything short of amazing. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419319i/831151._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4282657416929384131" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1503471419" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1503471419" />
    <a title="Summer Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14266988-summer-campbell"><img alt="Summer Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511432066p2/14266988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1503471419?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Summer Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Summer Campbell" href="/user/show/14266988-summer-campbell">Summer Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1503471419" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8572326703899632621"><b>I am sick to death of this romance genre. I have had enough. THIS IS IT. NO MORE OF THIS CONTEMPORARY <i>BULLSHIT</i>.</b><br/><br/>Admittedly, my favourite genre has always been romance. I have always, unexplainably, drifted to novels that feature a cute boy or a tortured hero. But I've decided I have to be more mature. I'm going to start reading books that actually have meaning, and depth, and are appropriate.<br/><br/>The problem is that there's a little trend going on here. A little trend that (if you read enough romance </span>
  <span id="freeText8572326703899632621" style="display:none"><b>I am sick to death of this romance genre. I have had enough. THIS IS IT. NO MORE OF THIS CONTEMPORARY <i>BULLSHIT</i>.</b><br /><br />Admittedly, my favourite genre has always been romance. I have always, unexplainably, drifted to novels that feature a cute boy or a tortured hero. But I've decided I have to be more mature. I'm going to start reading books that actually have meaning, and depth, and are appropriate.<br /><br />The problem is that there's a little trend going on here. A little trend that (if you read enough romance novels) you can easily pick up on. It goes a little something like this:<br /><br />1. Cute/beautiful girl enters as main character. Is woefully unaware that she is gorgeous/intelligent. Usually has domestic job such as being a baker (usually always likes cooking) a bartender, waitress, manager, photographer, sales assistant, interior designer etc... Lives in cutesy apartment. Has 1-3 BFFL's (Best Friends For Life). In later books in the series, these BFFL's usually hook up with the guy's BFFL's (note how they usually have the same amount of BFFL's). 0 -10%<br /><br />2. Enter hot guy. Preferably tall and gorgeous. Works at high profile/high salary job (he always earns more than the heroine.) Likes sports. Drives a nice car. Lives in a condo. Has the "I don't do relationship's - I fuck" attitude going on. 10% - 15%<br /><br />3. Cute girl and hot guy meet. Insta-lust occurs. He is suddenly weakened by her pretty face, and is turned on by the fact that she <b>thinks</b> she isn't anything special. He denies his feelings though. She thinks he's too good for her and lies down... and rolls over. 15%-20%<br /><br />4. Sexual tension. 20%-50%<br /><br />5. Lots of sex. 50% - 80%<br /><br />6. They realise the have feelings for each other and separate due to large cases of stupidity. 80%-90%.<br /><br />7. Due to BFFL's yelling at them, seeing the opposite with another partner or a long- awaited epiphany, characters reunite 90% of the way through the book. Cue makeup sex. Cue next BFFL's book.<br /><br />Now that that's over let me tell you what was wrong with this book. He's a dick. She's a ho. It's cheesy and follows the plot outlined above.^ It was in this particular scene though, that I had to put the book down and walk away.<br /><br />Hudson is the love interest.<br />Mira is Hudson's brother and owns a fashions boutique (see what I mean about domestic jobs!?)<br />Stacy is her sales assistant<br /><br />Look at how BITCHY this is!!!!!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>A tall, skinny blonde appeared out of an office in the back. She took the clothing Mira handed her. “Which room do you want to use?” Although she spoke to Mira, Stacy stared longingly toward Hudson. Longingly enough to make me wonder if they had a history or if Stacy wished they had a history. <br /><br />When Stacy had retreated out of earshot, I leaned into Mira. “Your assistant seems not to like me very much.” I paused. Should I say more? I decided yes. It was the real me that wanted to know about Stacy and Hudson, but girlfriend me would want to know too. “And she seems to like Hudson an awful lot. Is there something between them?”<br /><br />Mira hesitated, not looking me in the eye. “Ignore her. Stacy’s totally been in love with Huds for forever, even though she’s completely not his type. Nothing to worry about. It’s actually comical.”<br /><br />She seemed like she may have been holding back, but on the other hand, maybe she was just awkward about talking girl crushes with her brother’s girlfriend. I decided on the latter when Mira lowered her voice. “Did you notice how Hudson didn’t even give her the time of day?” She giggled.<br /><br />“I did.” I giggled too. For real. I liked Mira.</i>
</b><br /><br />What... so someone else is attracted to Hudson? That's not her fault. She's done nothing to you. What a ho.<br /><br />So that's it from me. If you have any books recommendations please tell me! I do like a little bit of romance in it, but at least half the plot should be based on another genre. Please. I'll take anything.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8572326703899632621" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_673242224" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/673242224" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/673242224?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=paperbacks">paperbacks</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer673242224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5959642348356805962"><br/><b>***4.5 stars***</b><br/><br/>It's been a while since I've read a billionaire story, and I'm glad that Hudson Pierce is the one to welcome me back into the genre with a talented, thick cock.....I mean, open arms! <br/><br/>The arrangement is simple: Hudson and Alayna will pretend to date so Hudson's bitch ass mama can think he's "capable" of love and stop trying to marry him off to his "best friend" Celia. He clearly understands his shortcomings and knows he truly is incapable, so of course this will work. Throw in his </span>
  <span id="freeText5959642348356805962" style="display:none"><br><b>***4.5 stars***</b><br><br>It's been a while since I've read a billionaire story, and I'm glad that Hudson Pierce is the one to welcome me back into the genre with a talented, thick cock.....I mean, open arms! <br><br>The arrangement is simple: Hudson and Alayna will pretend to date so Hudson's bitch ass mama can think he's "capable" of love and stop trying to marry him off to his "best friend" Celia. He clearly understands his shortcomings and knows he truly is incapable, so of course this will work. Throw in his past track record of manipulating woman for fun and well, we've got ourselves a damaged hero ladies. <br><br>Sex is on the table....but that's strictly to scratch an itch and in no way has bearing on the sham relationship. Don't confuse the two Alayna. We know you suffer from an obsessive disorder and need to be loved, which leads to stalking tendencies and hell, let's throw some restraining orders in there. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385388028ra/7138362.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Quite the fucked up pair these two make. One is obsessed with love and the other is incapable of it. Kind of like 1+1=74?<br><br>Doesn't that just sound like a cliche book waiting to happen. Yet, in no way, shape or form does it play out like that. The book is oddly refreshing with its honesty. I could not put it down and read it in one day!<br><br>There are no dumb misunderstandings or long soliloquies going on and on about how broken the characters are.....they just are. It's rooted in every gesture.<br><br>I REALLY thought Alayna was going to drive me crazy with her OCD. That was my one true hesitation with this series. Especially thinking she could handle an arrangement like this. Seriously, woman, you've had restraining orders against you from men way less awesome than Hudson! Hello!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385388585ra/7138508.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I LOVED her! She understood her triggers. She thought her feelings through. Yes, she had a couple of outbursts, but once she calmed, she quickly realized where her thoughts took her, apologized and explained her actions. Look at that....an adult! <br><br>Since we don't get Hudson's POV, you have to read between the lines to gauge where his head is at. And there is a lot to unravel with him. This first book is just scratching the surface. One thing I will say, I like how he handles Alayna. He respects her thoughts, values her mind and intelligence and craves her body. Ummmmm, yes...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385388027ra/7138361.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I'm drawn to you, Alayna. Not because I want to hurt you or make you feel a certain way, but because you're beautiful and sexy and smart and, yes, a little crazy, maybe, but you're not broken. And that makes me hopeful. <i>For me.</i>"</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384355073ra/6856783.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book doesn't end on a cliffy, but a good place to put a pause. There's still so much story to be told. Progress has been made, but the journey isn't done yet. Thankfully, I can dive right into the next book.....which I'll be doing immediately. <br><br>Celia, I've got my eye on you! Frankly, I think...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385388585ra/7138509.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

</b><br><br>Normally, when I reread books for a second time, I <u>tend</u> to usually lower my rating by a couple of stars. Why? Well, because I notice more mistakes and flaws about the book that I didn't catch when reading it the first time. This is one of the few books that after rereading, I love it even more!<br><br><b>
